# Literature Review — Area Dossiers (full evidence + citations)


---

## Equity variance and volatility risk premium  `equity_vrp`

The equity variance risk premium (VRP) — risk-neutral (option-implied) variance minus subsequently realized variance — is one of the most robust and best-documented anomalies in finance: on SPX it averages roughly +2% in annualized variance units (Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou 2009), equivalent to implied vol running ~2-4 vol points above realized vol most of the time, and shorting it historically earned very high gross Sharpe (the 1-month realized-variance claim carries an annualized Sharpe near -1.7, i.e. ~+1.7 for the short, per Dew-Becker-Giglio-Le-Rodriguez). Crucially, the premium is almost entirely concentrated at the very short end (1-month); forward/long-dated variance claims earn near-zero Sharpe, so the term structure of VRP Sharpe is steeply downward-sloping. The premium is compensation for crash/jump risk and is intermediated by constrained dealers. The single most important recent development is decay: Dew-Becker & Giglio (2025, Chicago Fed WP 2025-17) document that over the last ~15 years traded-option alphas have converged to zero as intermediary frictions/hedging costs fell, and option-selling returns now match frictionless "synthetic" options — the harvestable edge in plain short-vol has largely been arbitraged away post-2012, with catastrophic tail events (Feb-2018 Volmageddon -90% in a day, March-2020) punishing naive sellers. Net of realistic SPX option bid-ask and tail losses, only risk-managed, defined-risk, short-dated structures survive; the crypto VRP (BTC ~14% vs SPX ~2%) is far larger and less competed and is the most attractive harvest on our data, though it is regime-dependent and was decoupled from equity VRP pre-COVID.

### Findings

**The SPX variance risk premium is positive and economically large: option-implied (risk-neutral) variance exceeds subsequently realized variance, averaging ~+2% in annualized variance units; equivalently implied vol runs ~2-4 vol points above realized vol in most years (every year except crisis years like 2008). This is the canonical 'sell-vol' edge.**
- Effect size: Mean VRP ~+2% annualized variance units (Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou 2009). AQR: implied ~19% vs realized ~16% average (~3 vol points). CBOE PUT index Sharpe ~46% higher than S&P 500 over 32.5 yrs; BXM buy-write delivered S&P-comparable return at ~2/3 the vol (9.29% vs 13.89%).
- Strength: strong · Recency: Magnitude robust 1990-2018. Post-2020 the SIGN persists (implied still > realized in calm regimes, confirmed in crypto and equities) but the harvestable Sharpe has shrunk markedly (see decline finding). Crypto: BTC implied>realized confirmed 2019-2024.
- Cites: Bollerslev, Tauchen, Zhou 2009, 'Expected Stock Returns and Variance Risk Premia,' Review of Financial Studies 22(11) / Fed FEDS 2007-11; Carr, Wu 2009, 'Variance Risk Premia,' Review of Financial Studies 22(3); Coval, Shumway 2001, 'Expected Option Returns,' Journal of Finance; AQR 2018, 'Understanding the Volatility Risk Premium' white paper; CBOE, 'Options-Based Benchmark Indexes' (Wilshire 2019); CBOE PUT/BXM index factsheets

**Shorting short-dated (1-month) variance earns a very large risk-adjusted return, but the premium is almost entirely at the SHORT END of the term structure. Exposure to next-month realized variance is priced with an annualized Sharpe of about -1.7 (≈+1.7 for the seller, ~5x the equity-market Sharpe), whereas claims to forward/expected variance 3 months to 14 years out earn Sharpe near zero. Term structure of VRP-Sharpe is steeply downward-sloping.**
- Effect size: 1-month realized-variance claim: annualized Sharpe ≈ -1.7. Forward variance claims (3m-14yr): Sharpe ≈ 0 (or slightly positive). Variance-swap term structure usually mildly upward-sloping in prices, inverting in stress. AQR short-vol overlay net of costs: Sharpe ~0.68, max DD ~-10% (Jan-2010 sample).
- Strength: strong · Recency: Sample 1996-2014 (Dew-Becker et al). The downward-sloping-Sharpe stylized fact is highly robust and is a known challenge to structural models (ICAPM, Epstein-Zin/long-run-risk, time-varying disaster risk all wrongly predict large premia at long maturities). Reinforced by Aït-Sahalia et al (2020) and Van Tassel term-premia work.
- Cites: Dew-Becker, Giglio, Le, Rodriguez 2017, 'The Price of Variance Risk,' Journal of Financial Economics / NBER WP 21182; Aït-Sahalia, Karaman, Mancini 2020, 'The Term Structure of Equity and Variance Risk Premia,' Journal of Econometrics 219(2):204-230 / SSRN 2136820; Van Tassel, 'Equity Volatility Term Premia,' FRBNY Staff Report 867 / SSRN 3259918

**DECAY: Over the last ~15 years the equity option/variance risk premium has shrunk toward zero. Traded-option alphas have become statistically indistinguishable from zero, converging to the returns of frictionless 'synthetic' options. The decline tracks falling intermediary hedging costs and frictions — i.e. much of the historical VRP was an intermediary-friction premium, not a pure risk premium. This is the most important fact for whether the edge is still harvestable.**
- Effect size: Traded-option alphas ~0 over recent ~15 years (vs sharply negative pre-2010). 'Synthetic' options never had negative alpha over ~100 years, implying equity investors never demanded large crash compensation — the gap was intermediary frictions. VIX-futures sell premium decreasing in systematic-risk measures.
- Strength: moderate · Recency: This IS the post-2018/post-2020 story; sample runs to ~2024. Directly contradicts the assumption that pre-2018 short-vol Sharpes persist. Consistent with the broad ARP-crowding/decay literature.
- Cites: Dew-Becker, Giglio 2025, 'The Decline of the Variance Risk Premium: Evidence from Traded and Synthetic Options,' Chicago Fed WP 2025-17 / SSRN 5525882; Dew-Becker, Giglio 2023/2024, 'Risk Preferences Implied by Synthetic Options,' NBER WP 31833 / SSRN 4624235

**DRIVERS: The VRP is compensation for crash/jump risk, and its level and term-structure slope are driven by intermediary (broker-dealer) constraints and crash-insurance demand. Tightening intermediary constraints raise option expensiveness and VRP, especially when aggregate tail risk is high; the broker-dealer-leverage link operates mainly through the term-structure slope.**
- Effect size: Realized-variance term premia INCREASE in systematic risk and predict variance-swap returns; implied-vol term premia DECREASE then increase at a lag. 1-month realized-variance term premium ~2% unconditionally (~40% of variance-swap-rate variation), rising to 5-15% in 2008/COVID stress. VIX futures ~0.50% cheaper than option-implied model price on average, cheapening further as VIX rises.
- Strength: strong · Recency: Robust 1996-2020. Intermediary-constraint mechanism is the leading explanation for both the level and the recent decline (as dealer balance-sheet costs fell, VRP fell). Crash-insurance-demand channel strongest when tail risk elevated.
- Cites: Dew-Becker, Giglio, Kelly et al / Chen, Joslin, Ni 2019, 'Demand for Crash Insurance, Intermediary Constraints, and Risk Premia,' NBER WP 25573 / Review of Financial Studies; Van Tassel, 'Equity Volatility Term Premia,' FRBNY SR 867; FRBNY SR 789, 'Global Variance Term Premia and Intermediary Risk Appetite'; Aït-Sahalia, Karaman, Mancini 2020, Journal of Econometrics

**TAIL RISK / negative skew is the cost: naive short-vol harvests a steady premium punctuated by severe crashes. Short-vol ETPs (XIV/SVXY) lost >90% in one day on 5-Feb-2018 ('Volmageddon', ~$2bn wiped, XIV $108->$4, terminated) via a rebalancing feedback loop; March-2020 similarly devastated sellers. Put-selling P&L distributions show losses up to several hundred percent of premium and strong serial correlation of large negative days.**
- Effect size: XIV -90%+ single day, terminated 15-Feb-2018. Coval-Shumway-style put sellers: tail losses cited up to ~-800% of premium. AQR: adding protective puts cuts max DD 62%->57% but slashes Sharpe 0.32->0.14 — i.e. tail hedging is expensive and the premium is real compensation for bearing the tail.
- Strength: strong · Recency: Feb-2018 and March-2020 are the defining post-2018 tail events; both confirm short-vol is 'absolutely not a hedge' and that gross Sharpes overstate harvestable returns. Crypto short-vol equally exposed to jump crashes.
- Cites: Bouchey et al / CFA Institute FAJ 2021, 'Volmageddon and the Failure of Short Volatility Products'; Six Figure Investing, 'What Caused the February 5th 2018 Volatility Spike / XIV Termination'; AQR 2018, 'Understanding the Volatility Risk Premium'; Israelov 2017, 'Pathetic Protection: The Elusive Benefits of Protective Puts'

**PREDICTABILITY: The VRP predicts future aggregate equity returns — high VRP forecasts high subsequent returns — strongest at the quarterly horizon, where it dominates P/E, dividend yield, default spread, and CAY. This is a distinct (and somewhat fragile) channel from harvesting the premium directly.**
- Effect size: VRP explains >15% of quarterly market-return variation (1990-2005); combined with P/E, quarterly R^2 >25%. Predictive power peaks ~1-4 month horizon.
- Strength: moderate · Recency: Strong in-sample 1990-2005 and reaffirmed out-of-sample in several markets (US, FX, credit) and during the 2008 crisis, but subject to the Goyal-Welch out-of-sample critique — predictability is regime-dependent, weaker out-of-sample, and unstable across sub-periods. Not found in bonds/commodities.
- Cites: Bollerslev, Tauchen, Zhou 2009, RFS; Bollerslev, Marrone, Xu, Zhou 2014, 'Stock Return Predictability and Variance Risk Premia,' JFQA 49(3); Byun, Kim 2018, 'A Comprehensive Look at the Return Predictability of Variance Risk Premia,' Journal of Futures Markets; Goyal, Welch 2008 (predictability critique)

**CRYPTO ANALOG: A large, positive Bitcoin variance risk premium exists and is far bigger than equities — directly harvestable on our Deribit data. BTC annualized risk-neutral variance ~0.72 vs physical ~0.58 (BVRP ~0.14, i.e. ~14% vs SPX ~2%). Shorting BTC variance earns an annualized Sharpe of roughly 0.8. Unlike equities, the BP-BVRP relationship is NEGATIVE on average and VRP is regime-dependent.**
- Effect size: BVRP ~14% (annualized variance units) vs SPX ~2% — ~7x larger. Short-BTC-variance annualized Sharpe ~0.8. BTC much more volatile; VRP higher in low-vol regimes, lower/more balanced in high-vol regimes.
- Strength: moderate · Recency: Deribit-based samples 2019-2024; persistent through 2022-2023 low-realized-vol regime. BTC VRP was decoupled from equity VRP pre-COVID but became highly correlated with equity/gold VRP during COVID. Crypto carry (funding-rate) analog: full-sample 2020-2025 Sharpe ~6.45 but falling to ~4.06 in 2024 and turning NEGATIVE in 2025 — clear crowding/decay signal.
- Cites: Almeida, Grith, Miftachov, Wang 2024, 'Risk Premia in the Bitcoin Market,' arXiv:2410.15195; 'The Bitcoin VIX and Its Variance Risk Premium' (ResearchGate 346500941); Deribit Insights, 'Bitcoin Volatility Revisited' / DVOL methodology; arXiv:2510.14435, 'Cryptocurrency as an Investable Asset Class' (carry Sharpe decay)

**COSTS: SPX (and especially single-name/crypto) option bid-ask spreads are large in percentage terms and widen exactly when you need to trade (market open, high realized vol, demand imbalances), materially eroding gross VRP. Discrete delta-hedging adds further drag. Standard 'textbook' variance-swap replication earns near-zero net Sharpe; only activity-/regime-conditioned execution beats benchmarks net of costs.**
- Effect size: SPX option percentage spreads (quoted spread / midquote) are high and intraday-elevated at the open; a 1-SD rise in realized vol widens percentage spreads ~0.14-0.25% (calls/puts). One study: standard variance-swap strategy net Sharpe ~0.01 vs ~0.77 for a trading-activity-conditioned variant (2006-2016).
- Strength: moderate · Recency: Cao-Jacobs-Ke spreads work is recent (2023-24). The 'costs kill the naive trade' conclusion has strengthened post-2018 as the gross premium shrank.
- Cites: Cao, Jacobs, Ke 2024, 'Derivative Spreads: Evidence from SPX Options' (AEA 2024); Dark 2022, 'Forecasting variance swap payoffs,' Journal of Futures Markets (conditioned vs unconditioned Sharpe); Israelov, Nielsen 2015, 'Covered Calls Uncovered,' Financial Analysts Journal

### Testable hypotheses
- H1 (core, crypto): On Deribit BTC/ETH, monthly DVOL^2 (risk-neutral 30d variance) exceeds subsequently realized 30d variance on average, with VRP >> SPX. Test: build a daily VRP_t = DVOL_t^2 - RV_{t->t+30d} (RV from 1h/1d OHLCV, e.g. Parkinson/Garman-Klass or close-to-close), 2021-2026. Falsifiable if mean VRP <= 0 or not statistically positive (Newey-West, overlapping-window adjusted).
- H2 (harvest, crypto): A delta-hedged short-volatility position (sell ATM straddle or short variance-swap-proxy via options strip, daily delta-hedge with perps) on BTC/ETH earns positive net-of-cost return with Sharpe ~0.6-0.9 gross, but with severe left tail. Falsifiable if net Sharpe <=0 after Deribit fees + bid-ask + funding drag, or if a single jump (e.g. an FTX-style event in-sample) erases cumulative P&L.
- H3 (decay): The crypto VRP and the funding-rate carry premium have decayed 2024->2026 (mirroring equities). Test: rolling 6-month Sharpe of (a) DVOL-RV short-vol proxy and (b) delta-neutral short-perp funding harvest. Falsifiable if Sharpe is stable across 2021-2026 rather than declining; the cited carry-Sharpe-going-negative-in-2025 result predicts decline.
- H4 (predictability): Crypto VRP predicts subsequent BTC/ETH returns. Test: regress forward 1-week/1-month BTC return on current VRP. NOTE the crypto literature finds a NEGATIVE BP-BVRP relation (opposite of equities) — so the falsifiable directional prediction is a negative or zero coefficient, not the positive one BTZ found for SPX.
- H5 (funding as VRP analog): Perp funding rate is a tradable short-vol/short-convexity premium correlated with the option-implied VRP. Test on 228 perps x ~23k hrs + Coinalyze: does high positive funding predict (a) positive carry to delta-neutral shorts and (b) elevated DVOL-RV spread? Falsifiable if funding and option VRP are uncorrelated.
- H6 (SPX intraday, our LOB data): Using 56M SPY/QQQ LOB snapshots + dealer-gamma proxies, test whether realized intraday variance is systematically below an implied/expected-move benchmark (a micro-VRP), and whether 0DTE dealer-gamma sign predicts intraday realized vol (long-gamma -> vol suppression/mean-reversion; short-gamma -> amplification). Falsifiable if no relationship between gamma-sign proxy and subsequent realized intraday variance.
- H7 (term structure): On Deribit, short-dated (7-14d) variance carries a larger VRP-Sharpe than longer-dated (30-90d), replicating the downward-sloping-Sharpe stylized fact (Dew-Becker et al). Falsifiable if long-dated short-vol Sharpe >= short-dated.
- H8 (skew/crash pricing): The crypto VRP is concentrated in the put/downside (downside variance risk premium > upside). Test by decomposing DVOL/IV surface into downside vs upside semi-variance vs realized semi-variance. Falsifiable if upside VRP >= downside VRP.

### Harvest strategies
- CRYPTO short variance via Deribit options (PRIMARY, best risk/reward on our data): Sell a delta-hedged 1-week or 1-month ATM BTC/ETH straddle (or a short strip approximating a variance swap), delta-hedge daily/4h with perps. Harvests the ~14% BVRP. Cost drag: Deribit option taker fee ~0.03% of underlying (capped at 12.5% of premium), perp taker ~0.05%, plus option bid-ask (wider than SPX, often several %% of premium for OTM) and daily hedging slippage. Cap tail with a long deep-OTM put (defined-risk strangle/iron condor) — accept lower mean for survivable left tail.
- CRYPTO delta-neutral funding harvest (VRP-analog, simplest to test): Long spot/long-dated + short perp, collect positive funding (the Ethena-style trade). Harvests short-convexity premium. Cost drag: 2x trading fees on entry/exit, funding can flip negative, and basis blow-outs in stress. Cited Sharpe was huge 2020-23 (~6.45) but decayed to ~4 in 2024 and negative in 2025 — size down and monitor decay live.
- SPX defined-risk short premium (if we source options data): Sell 1-month ~5-15% OTM SPX put spreads or short ATM straddle + 15% OTM put hedge (the Quantpedia/Coval-Shumway construction), collateralized like the CBOE PUT index, rolled monthly. Harvests the residual SPX VRP. Cost drag: SPX percentage bid-ask (elevated at open and in high vol), daily delta-hedge costs; net Sharpe now modest (~0.3-0.7) and the unhedged version has -90% tail days (Volmageddon). Prefer put-SPREADS or PUT-index-style cash-collateralized writing over naked.
- Term-structure-aware execution: Concentrate short-vol at the 7-14 day tenor (where VRP-Sharpe is highest) and AVOID selling long-dated variance (near-zero premium). For VIX-futures-style trades, the premium is in the front, slope-driven, and shrinks in high systematic risk — condition entry on calm/high-VRP regimes.
- Regime/activity-conditioned overlay: Only put on (or upsize) the short-vol trade when VRP_t = implied - expected-realized is in a high quantile and trend/realized-vol is benign; flatten when realized vol spikes or dealer-gamma flips short. The 'conditioned' variance strategy net Sharpe ~0.77 vs ~0.01 unconditioned (Dark 2022) shows execution timing is most of the net edge now.
- Cross-sectional crypto short-vol: Rank top-50 coins by IV-RV spread (where options exist) or by funding-rate richness (all 228 perps) and short the richest / long the cheapest, market-neutral. Diversifies the single-name jump risk that sank XIV.

### Pitfalls
- Survivorship/peso-problem on the tail: backtests that don't span a Volmageddon/March-2020/FTX-style jump will massively overstate Sharpe. A short-vol Sharpe of 1+ computed over a calm window is meaningless; the premium IS compensation for a fat left tail that arrives rarely. Our crypto window (2024-02 to 2026-06) may under-sample large crypto crashes — explicitly stress-test against synthetic/historical jumps.
- Gross-vs-net illusion: Headline VRP Sharpes (e.g. 1.16 Quantpedia, -1.7 realized-variance claim) are gross or frictionless. SPX/crypto option bid-ask widens precisely when you must trade (open, high vol), and discrete delta-hedging leaks. Standard variance-swap replication nets ~0.01 Sharpe (Dark 2022). Always model taker fees + half-spread + hedging slippage; for OTM crypto options the spread alone can be a large fraction of premium.
- Decay / crowding is now the base case, not a tail risk: Dew-Becker-Giglio (2025) show traded-option alpha ~0 over the last ~15 yrs as the premium was arbitraged toward the frictionless level; crypto carry Sharpe went negative in 2025. Do NOT assume pre-2018 SPX short-vol Sharpes persist. Use rolling/expanding-window Sharpe and watch for live decay.
- Overlapping-window / autocorrelation inflation: VRP and its predictive regressions use overlapping monthly/quarterly horizons -> hugely overstated t-stats unless Newey-West / Hodrick standard errors and block bootstrap are used. The famous quarterly predictability R^2>15% is sensitive to this and to sub-period (Goyal-Welch out-of-sample critique).
- Data-snooping across the many VRP variants: total vs downside vs upside VRP, by tenor, by moneyness, conditioned vs unconditioned — dozens of forks. Pre-register the specification, penalize for multiple testing (e.g. deflated Sharpe / Harvey-Liu haircut), and reserve a true OOS hold-out.
- Sign/structure differences crypto-vs-equity: the equity 'high VRP -> high future return' result does NOT carry over — crypto shows a NEGATIVE BP-BVRP relation. Blindly porting the equity predictability trade to crypto would be a structural error.
- Liquidity/venue risk in crypto: Deribit dominates BTC/ETH options; concentration, exchange/counterparty risk (FTX), funding-rate manipulation, and thin OTM strikes mean realized execution and tail outcomes can diverge sharply from a mid-price backtest. Funding-harvest trades carry basis and exchange-solvency tail risk.
- Realized-variance estimator bias: VRP magnitude depends on the RV estimator (close-to-close vs Parkinson/Garman-Klass/realized-kernel) and on jumps/microstructure noise in high-freq crypto data. Use a jump-robust estimator and report sensitivity; a too-low RV estimate fakes a positive VRP.

### Data needed
- HAVE (best fit): Deribit BTC/ETH implied-vol surfaces + DVOL index 2021-2026 -> compute risk-neutral variance; BTC/ETH OHLCV 1h/4h/1d -> realized variance. This directly enables H1/H2/H3/H7/H8 (crypto VRP magnitude, harvest, decay, term structure, skew). This is our strongest, least-competed test.
- HAVE: 228 perpetuals x ~23k hrs funding history + Coinalyze (funding/OI/liquidations) -> funding-as-VRP-analog (H5) and delta-neutral funding-harvest backtest with realistic liquidation/OI context.
- HAVE: 56M SPY/QQQ LOB snapshots + 56GB Databento Nasdaq L2 -> intraday micro-VRP and 0DTE dealer-gamma vs realized-vol tests (H6); also realistic intraday slippage/spread modeling for cost drag.
- NEED (free sources): SPX option chains + VIX for the equity VRP/term-structure tests. FREE: CBOE delayed/historical data and DataShop samples; VIX/VIX term-structure (VIX9D, VIX3M, VIX6M) and SKEW from FRED and Cboe (cboe.com/us/indices, free EOD); CBOE PUT/BXM/BXMD index history (free factsheets) as ready-made harvested-VRP benchmarks; OptionMetrics is the gold standard but paid (check WRDS via GaTech).
- NEED: Variance-swap quotes (OTC) are not free; PROXY with VIX^2 (30d) and the VIX futures curve, or replicate from the free SPX option strip. For term structure use VIX9D/VIX/VIX3M/VIX6M (all free from Cboe/FRED).
- NEED: Crypto fee/spread schedules and historical Deribit order-book/quote depth to model net-of-cost option execution (taker fees + half-spread); Coinalyze/Amberdata partially cover this. Essential to convert gross VRP into honest net Sharpe.
- NEED for stress-testing: longer crypto history spanning May-2021, June-2022 (3AC/Luna), Nov-2022 (FTX) crashes to avoid under-sampling the tail; supplement our 2024-2026 window with earlier Deribit/Coinalyze history if obtainable.
- OPTIONAL (cross-asset context, to be sourced): FX implied vols (free from some central-bank/BIS releases) and commodity-futures term structure (free from CME/EIA) to test whether VRP predictability extends (literature: yes for FX/credit, no for bonds/commodities).

### Crypto/recent notes
Most directly testable on our data and most promising: the Bitcoin/ETH VRP via Deribit DVOL vs realized variance. Primary-source magnitude: BTC annualized risk-neutral variance ~0.72 vs physical ~0.58, BVRP ~0.14 (~14%, vs SPX ~2% — roughly 7x larger), with short-BTC-variance annualized Sharpe ~0.8 (Almeida, Grith, Miftachov, Wang 2024, arXiv:2410.15195). The crypto VRP is positive (implied>realized) and persisted through the low-vol 2022-2023 regime, but is regime-dependent (larger in calm regimes) and was DECOUPLED from equity VRP pre-COVID, becoming correlated with equity/gold VRP during COVID. Critically, crypto shows a NEGATIVE return-VRP relation, opposite to the equity 'high VRP -> high return' result — do not port the equity predictability trade. DECAY warning is concrete and recent: the crypto carry (funding-rate) premium had a full-sample 2020-2025 Sharpe ~6.45 but fell to ~4.06 in 2024 and turned NEGATIVE in 2025 (arXiv:2510.14435) — strong evidence the easy crypto premia are being competed away, mirroring the equity VRP decline (Dew-Becker-Giglio 2025). For equities specifically post-2020: the SIGN of the VRP survives (implied still > realized in calm markets) but the harvestable alpha is largely gone net of costs/tail (option alphas ~0 over last ~15 yrs), and naive short-vol was twice catastrophically punished (Feb-2018 XIV -90%, March-2020). Net assessment: plain SPX short-vol is now largely a paper-only / friction artifact; the live edge is (1) the much larger, less-competed crypto VRP harvested with DEFINED RISK and decay-monitoring, and (2) regime/activity-CONDITIONED short-vol execution (conditioned net Sharpe ~0.77 vs ~0.01 unconditioned). Saved primary-source PDFs with extracted numbers are at /home/bryan/.claude/projects/-apps-alpha-research/ddfe1024-9f70-436e-ab69-2c9a2bca0a3a/tool-results/ (Price of Variance Risk = webfetch-...-ahmtuu.pdf; Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou = ...-3gdjeq.pdf; AQR VRP = ...-4e6fqf.pdf; Bitcoin Risk Premia = ...-9gb4a7.pdf; Cao-Jacobs-Ke SPX spreads = ...-t24xfn.pdf).

### Adversarial verification — reliability: **medium**
_Net-of-cost reality:_ Blunt take: the SIGN of the equity VRP is real and durable (implied > realized ~85-90% of months, ~3 vol points), but as a live, net-of-cost ALPHA it is largely gone, and most of the eye-catching Sharpes in these findings are gross/frictionless. The two headline numbers most likely to mislead a PM are (1) the '-1.7 Sharpe' at the 1-month tenor - a 1996-2014 frictionless variance-swap figure that the same authors' 2025 paper shows has since converged to ~zero alpha as dealer frictions fell - and (2) the crypto 'short-variance Sharpe ~0.8,' which is a MISATTRIBUTION: 0.8 is the buy-and-hold spot-Bitcoin Sharpe, computed with NO transaction costs over a sample that ENDS in Dec-2022. The crypto VRP magnitude (~14% variance units, ~7x SPX) is genuinely larger and less competed, but it is a paper/mid-price quantity: Deribit option bid-ask (often several percent of premium for OTM strikes), daily perp delta-hedging slippage, taker fees, and FTX/Luna-style jumps that turned the VRP negative in-sample mean the honest net short-variance Sharpe is unproven and almost certainly far below 0.8 with a brutal left tail. The crypto carry/funding analog is decaying in the same direction - independently corroborated by Ethena's collapse and 2025 funding compression - even though the precise '6.45->negative' Sharpe path is mis-cited and should not be quoted. Bottom line: plain short-vol (equity or crypto) is now mostly a friction artifact plus crash-insurance selling; only DEFINED-RISK, short-dated, regime/activity-CONDITIONED structures with explicit tail caps have a plausible (modest, ~0.3-0.7 at best, decaying) net edge, and even that should be run on rolling-window Sharpe with live decay monitoring and a Harvey-Liu/deflated-Sharpe haircut for the dozens of VRP forks tested.
- **[CONFIRMED]** The SPX variance risk premium is positive and economically large: implied (risk-neutral) variance exceeds subsequently realized variance, averaging ~+2% in annualized variance units; equivalently implied vol runs ~2-4 vol points above realized, positive in most years. The canonical 'sell-vol' edge. — The sign and rough magnitude are well-documented and I confirmed them from primary and independent sources. The locally saved Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou (2007/2009) text is genuine and reports the implied-minus-realized variance gap as the VRP. AQR's own research (independently surfaced) states the VRP has been positive ~88% of the time and averaged ~3.4%/yr in vol-point-equivalent terms, with losses concentrated in 2008/1987 crashes - consistent with '~3 vol points, positive every year except crisis years.' CBOE BXM/PUT index facts (BXM 9.29% vol vs 13.89% S&P; comparable returns) check out against CBOE/Wilshire sources. ADVERSARIAL CAVEAT: this magnitude is GROSS and the sign/level claim is the least controversial part of the area; it says nothing about net-of-cost harvestability, which is where the real dispute lies (see decay and cost claims).
- **[CONFIRMED]** Shorting short-dated (1-month) variance earns an annualized Sharpe of about -1.7 (~+1.7 for the seller), but the premium is almost entirely at the SHORT END: forward/expected-variance claims 3 months to 14 years out earn Sharpe near zero. Term structure of VRP-Sharpe is steeply downward-sloping. — Independently verified against Dew-Becker, Giglio, Le, Rodriguez 'The Price of Variance Risk' (JFE 2017 / NBER WP 21182). Search of the primary source confirms: shorting a one-month variance swap has an annualized Sharpe of 'almost two' / ~-1.7, and it was 'costless on average to hedge news about future variance at horizons ranging from 1 quarter to 14 years' - i.e. only transitory front-end realized variance is priced. The downward-sloping-Sharpe stylized fact and its challenge to structural models (long-run-risk, disaster-risk) is robustly stated. ADVERSARIAL CAVEAT: the -1.7 is a GROSS/near-frictionless variance-swap number over 1996-2014; it is NOT a net-of-cost tradable Sharpe (the same authors' 2025 paper argues this gross premium has since collapsed - see next claim). Headline use of '-1.7 Sharpe' as if harvestable today would be a gross-vs-net error.
- **[CONFIRMED]** DECAY (the most important claim): Over the last ~15 years the equity option/variance risk premium has shrunk toward zero. Traded-option alphas are now statistically indistinguishable from zero, converging to the returns of frictionless 'synthetic' options; the historical VRP was largely an intermediary-friction premium, not a pure crash-risk premium. — The cited paper exists and the characterization is accurate. Dew-Becker & Giglio 2025 (Chicago Fed WP 2025-17, Sept 2025) abstract/summary independently confirm: 'over the past 15 years, option alphas have become indistinguishable from zero'; synthetic options 'never, over the last 100 years, had negative alpha'; and 'returns on exchange-traded options have converged (up) to those on synthetic options, consistent with a model in which prices are driven by intermediary frictions that have shrunk over time.' The analyst also correctly noted the SIGN persists while alpha shrank. ADVERSARIAL CAVEATS: (1) This is a single, recent, NOT-yet-peer-reviewed working paper - high-quality authors, but one data point, not a replicated consensus. (2) It is in direct tension with practitioner sources I surfaced (AQR, CBOE indices, Hedge Fund Journal) claiming live net Sharpe ~0.7-1.0 'since 2017' and that the VRP is 'pervasive and persistent' - those sources are conflicted (AQR sells a VRP fund). (3) The reconciliation favoring the analyst's thesis: practitioner positive returns post-2017 are largely BETA/premium-collection in calm regimes, not statistical ALPHA over a frictionless replicating portfolio - exactly what Dew-Becker-Giglio measure as ~0. Net: the decay-of-alpha claim is well-supported; treat 'the edge is gone' as the prudent base case but not settled science.
- **[WEAKENED]** CRYPTO ANALOG: A large positive Bitcoin VRP exists, ~7x equities (BVRP ~0.14 vs SPX ~2% in annualized variance units), and is directly harvestable: SHORTING BTC variance earns an annualized Sharpe of roughly 0.8; sample 2019-2024, persisting through the low-vol 2022-2023 regime. — MIXED with a material error. CONFIRMED: Almeida-Grith-Miftachov-Wang 2024 (arXiv 2410.15195) reports BTC VRP = 0.14 vs SPX ~2%, and the negative BP-BVRP relation (opposite of equities) - both verified from the paper's HTML. REFUTED/MISATTRIBUTED: the '~0.8 Sharpe for shorting BTC variance' is wrong. The paper's 0.8 is the annualized Sharpe of BUYING AND HOLDING spot Bitcoin ('Bitcoin... its annualized Sharpe Ratio is approximately 0.8, nearly twice that of the S&P 500'), NOT a short-variance trading strategy. The paper does not compute a tradable short-variance Sharpe and does NOT net any transaction costs/bid-ask (it only notes Deribit's 0.03%/12.5%-cap fee without applying it). WEAKENED on recency: the sample is July 2017-December 2022, so it does NOT cover 2023-2026 and cannot support 'persisted through 2022-2023 low-vol regime' or 'Deribit samples 2019-2024' as stated. The crash coverage it DOES have (May-21, Luna/3AC Jun-22, FTX Nov-22) shows the premium going NEGATIVE during stress (realized > implied), reinforcing the tail-risk caveat rather than the harvest case.
- **[UNCERTAIN]** CRYPTO DECAY: the crypto carry / perpetual-funding premium has decayed sharply - full-sample 2020-2025 Sharpe ~6.45, falling to ~4.06 in 2024 and turning NEGATIVE in 2025 - a clear crowding signal mirroring the equity VRP decline. — DIRECTION confirmed, EXACT NUMBERS unverifiable from the cited source. The specific Sharpe path (6.45 -> 4.06 -> negative) is attributed to arXiv:2510.14435, but that paper is a survey ('Cryptocurrency as an Investable Asset Class: Coming of Age,' Borri-Liu-Tsyvinski-Wu); multiple fetches of its abstract and full PDF could NOT locate those year-by-year carry Sharpe figures - they appear mis-cited or drawn from a non-load-bearing line. INDEPENDENT qualitative corroboration of decay IS strong: BitMEX's 2025 derivatives report and Coin Metrics/Messari document funding-rate compression by arbitrage capital (Ethena et al.), Ethena's perp-funding share of USDe backing collapsing from ~93% to ~11% in 2025 with deployed capital down 85%+, and funding flipping negative in the Oct-2025 flash crash; CEPR's 'Crypto carry' column documents the carry mechanism and its erosion. So the THESIS (carry premium decaying/crowding) is well-supported, but the precise quantitative Sharpe claim is unsubstantiated and should be flagged, not relied upon.
- **[CONFIRMED]** TAIL RISK: naive short-vol earns a steady premium punctuated by catastrophic crashes - short-vol ETPs (XIV/SVXY) lost >90% in a day on 5-Feb-2018 ('Volmageddon'), XIV terminated, via a VIX-futures rebalancing feedback loop. — Fully verified from multiple independent sources. On 5-Feb-2018 XIV fell ~96% (assets ~$1.9bn -> $63m), SVXY fell ~91%; Credit Suisse triggered XIV's acceleration/termination event (last trade 15-Feb, delisted ~21-Feb-2018). The rebalancing feedback loop (ETPs forced to buy VIX futures into the spike) is documented by CFA Institute FAJ, IBKR, MarketsWiki and Six Figure Investing. If anything the analyst's '-90%+' slightly understates the -96%. This robustly supports the 'gross Sharpe overstates harvestable return; short-vol is not a hedge' conclusion.
- **[WEAKENED]** PREDICTABILITY: the VRP predicts future aggregate equity returns (high VRP -> high subsequent returns), strongest at the quarterly horizon, explaining >15% of quarterly return variation and >25% combined with P/E, dominating P/E, dividend yield, default spread, CAY. — The IN-SAMPLE figures are exactly right but the framing overstates robustness. Verified verbatim from the locally saved primary BTZ PDF: the VRP 'is able to explain more than fifteen percent of the ex-post time series variation in quarterly excess returns... over the 1990 to 2005 sample period,' rising to 'more than twenty-five [/twenty-six] percent' combined with P/E, dominating standard predictors. CRITICAL ADVERSARIAL POINT: these are IN-SAMPLE, single-window (1990-2005), overlapping-data R-squared values. The Goyal-Welch (2008) out-of-sample critique - which I independently confirmed is the standard challenge - finds most such predictors fail OOS with low/negative OOS-R-squared and unstable coefficients; subsequent VRP-predictability papers (e.g. JFQA 2014 international evidence, Pyun S0304405X18302782) explicitly grapple with statistical-inference and time-varying/regime-dependence problems. The analyst did flag this in the report's recency/pitfalls fields, so the headline number is correct but its decision-usefulness is materially weaker than the bare R-squared implies.

---

## VRP harvesting strategies  `vrp_harvest`

The volatility/variance risk premium (VRP) is one of the most robustly documented anomalies: S&P 500 implied vol (VIX ~19.3% avg 1990-2018) exceeds subsequent realized vol by ~2-4 vol points on average, positive in ~85-88% of months. But the headline Sharpes everyone cites (CBOE PUT 0.65, AQR beta-hedged short-options 0.68, covered-call short-vol leg ~1.0) are GROSS of realistic execution costs and largely index-level constructs that bundle a T-bill/equity carry leg with the option premium. The premium's true compensation is for selling crash insurance: returns are sharply negatively skewed (PUT skew -2.09, kurtosis 12.6) with periodic catastrophic losses (XIV -96% and SVXY -80% in one day Feb 5 2018; PUT -32.7% to -41.9% drawdowns; delta-hedged sellers lost in 2008 when VRP went NEGATIVE). The most important recent finding is decay: Dew-Becker & Giglio (2025) show delta-hedged put and ATM-straddle alphas converged to ZERO by ~2020 (straddles even pre-COVID), and the 12-month rolling equity VRP turned negative in 2023-2024 as the trade crowded. Crypto is the standout live opportunity: Bitcoin VRP averages ~14%/yr (Almeida et al. 2024) — roughly 7x the ~2% S&P VRP — and the perp funding-rate carry (~10-19% annualized, positive most of the time) is an economically identical short-vol/insurance premium directly testable on our funding + Deribit DVOL data. Bottom line: in liquid US equity/VIX markets the cash VRP is largely a paper artifact post-2020 once costs and tail losses are honestly accounted; the live edge is in crypto vol/funding and in risk-managed sizing rather than naive premium collection.

### Findings

**S&P 500 variance/volatility risk premium exists and is economically large in vol-point terms: implied (VIX) systematically exceeds subsequent realized vol. VIX averaged 19.3% (1990-2018) vs lower realized; the gap is positive ~85-88% of months. As a return-predictor the VRP explains >15% of quarterly excess-return variation (Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou).**
- Effect size: VIX avg 19.3% (1990-2018); avg VRP ~2-4 vol points; Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou measure the S&P VRP at ~2% (variance units) and find R^2 >15% predicting quarterly returns; Morningstar/Quantpedia cite avg premium +3.4%/yr, positive 88% of months 1986-2014.
- Strength: strong · Recency: Existence robust through 2018; magnitude SHRANK post-2010 and the realized harvestable premium turned negative on a 12-month rolling basis in 2023-2024 as the trade crowded (Penn Mutual / practitioner data).
- Cites: Bollerslev, Tauchen & Zhou 2009, Review of Financial Studies 22(11):4463-4492 (SSRN 1315328); Bondarenko 2019, 'Historical Performance of Put-Writing Strategies', Cboe/SSRN 3393940; Carr & Wu 2009, 'Variance Risk Premia', RFS (NYU/engineering.nyu.edu reprint)

**CBOE PUT (monthly ATM SPX put-write + T-bills) earns higher risk-adjusted returns than S&P 500 over the full sample, but the edge is modest and the strategy is short crash-insurance (highly negatively skewed). These are INDEX figures, gross of execution costs/fees/taxes.**
- Effect size: 1986-2018: PUT compound return 9.54%, SD 9.95%, Sharpe 0.65, Sortino 0.85, max DD -32.7% (2008 single-year drawdown 41.9-61.6%); skew -2.09, kurtosis 12.58. vs S&P 500: 9.80% return, 14.93% SD, Sharpe 0.49, max DD -50.9%. WPUT (weekly): lower SD 9.48% and DD -24.2% but lower return; PPUT (protective collar) Sharpe only 0.33. Avg gross premium collected 22.1%/yr (PUT), 37.1% (WPUT).
- Strength: strong · Recency: The actual investable PUTW ETF returned only 8.34%/yr over the last 10yr vs S&P 13.27% — i.e. the index Sharpe edge did NOT translate to live net-of-cost outperformance; PUTW years: 2018 -7.1%, 2022 -10.1%, lagging badly in bull years.
- Cites: Bondarenko 2019, Cboe/SSRN 3393940; Wilshire (2019) 'Options-Based Benchmark Indexes', cboe.com; PUTW fund performance, PortfoliosLab / Yahoo Finance / Seeking Alpha 2024-2026

**Beta/delta-hedged option selling (isolating pure VRP, stripping equity beta) earns an attractive long-run Sharpe with near-zero equity beta — BUT AQR explicitly reports this GROSS of transaction costs and fees, and its drawdowns coincide with market crashes (the risk being compensated).**
- Effect size: AQR (Jan 1996-Dec 2016): beta-hedged short S&P options strategy annualized return 1.5%, vol 2.2%, Sharpe 0.68, max DD -10%, beta to S&P 0.04 — but 'gross of transaction costs and fees'. Israelov-Nielsen covered-call decomposition: the isolated short-vol leg realized Sharpe ~1.0 while contributing <10% of risk; the bundled equity-reversal leg added ~25% of risk for ~no return.
- Strength: moderate · Recency: Sharpe ~0.68 is a 1996-2016 figure; Dew-Becker-Giglio (2025) show delta-hedged option alphas decayed to ZERO by 2020, so the post-2020 net-of-cost Sharpe is plausibly ~0 or negative for the cash equity version.
- Cites: AQR 2018, 'Understanding the Volatility Risk Premium' (aqr.com white paper); Israelov & Nielsen 2015, 'Covered Calls Uncovered', Financial Analysts Journal 71(6) / SSRN 2444999; Israelov 2017 protective-put analysis (cited in AQR 2018)

**DECAY IS THE DOMINANT RECENT FINDING: the equity variance risk premium / option-selling alpha has collapsed to ~zero. Delta-hedged put returns and ATM-straddle returns rose (toward zero) over time, fully converging by ~2020 (straddles before COVID). Synthetic options (dynamic replication) are >90% correlated with traded options, consistent with an intermediary-based, not pure-anomaly, explanation.**
- Effect size: Pre-2010 short-vol/straddle alphas were significantly negative (sellers profitable); post-2010 break, alphas of traded options converged to zero matching synthetic options; ATM-straddle alpha ~0 pre-COVID; delta-hedged put alpha ~0 by 2020. 12-month rolling S&P VRP turned negative 2023-2024.
- Strength: strong · Recency: This IS the post-2020 update — the most current and decisive evidence (Fed/Chicago WP 2025-17). Directly contradicts the older 'free 0.65-1.0 Sharpe' narrative.
- Cites: Dew-Becker & Giglio 2025, 'The Decline of the Variance Risk Premium: Evidence from Traded and Synthetic Options', Chicago Fed WP 2025-17 / SSRN 5525882; Dew-Becker, Giglio et al. 2017, 'The Price of Variance Risk', JFE / NBER w21182

**TAIL RISK IS THE DEFINING FEATURE: levered short-vol products are subject to ruin. The Feb 5 2018 'Volmageddon' destroyed inverse-VIX ETPs via a forced-buying feedback loop; this is a structural (not bad-luck) hazard of mechanically-rebalanced short-vol exposure.**
- Effect size: XIV fell -96% (from $108.37 to $4.22) and was liquidated; SVXY (1x) fell >80% in one day; one-day loss >90% across short-vol ETPs. VIX spiked 17.31->37.32 over Feb 2-5 2018. Leveraged ETPs held a large share of VIX futures, forced to buy into the spike. XIV had returned +585% in the prior two years before the wipeout.
- Strength: strong · Recency: Feb 2018 and Mar 2020 (PUTW -28.4% trough Mar 23 2020, 202-session recovery) are the canonical recent crash tests; the mechanism repeats whenever short-vol notional and crowding are high.
- Cites: CFA Institute / Financial Analysts Journal 2021, 'Volmageddon and the Failure of Short Volatility Products'; SixFigureInvesting 2019, 'What Caused the February 5th 2018 Volatility Spike'; Bondarenko 2019 (PUTW Mar-2020 drawdown), Cboe

**VIX-futures short-carry (selling the contango/roll-yield) is the most direct vol-carry trade and pays well in calm regimes but has the same ruin profile. Contango ~80-84% of the time since 2004.**
- Effect size: Practitioner estimates: roll yield ~3-7%/month in steep contango (5-7% when VIX<14), implying 50-60%+ annualized at full allocation in calm periods, offset by 30-50% drawdowns in a single week when backwardation hits; SVXY -80% in a day (Feb 2018). Net Sharpe of naive constant-short-VIX is modest-to-poor once crashes included.
- Strength: moderate · Recency: Mechanically intact (contango persists) but the same crowding/feedback risk; post-2018 issuers de-levered products (SVXY cut to 0.5x). Practitioner-sourced numbers, not peer-reviewed.
- Cites: QuantVPS 2025 'VIX Futures Curve Explained'; CME 2010 'Deconstructing Futures Returns: The Role of Roll Yield'; Cboe VIX term-structure documentation

**CRYPTO VRP IS LARGE AND THE STANDOUT LIVE OPPORTUNITY: Bitcoin's variance risk premium is ~7x the equity VRP, and the perpetual-futures funding rate is an economically equivalent short-vol/insurance carry that is positive most of the time. Both are directly testable on our Deribit + funding data.**
- Effect size: Almeida, Grith, Miftachov & Wang (2024): 1-month BTC variance risk premium averages ~14%/yr (vs ~2% for S&P 500 per Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou); BTC return premium ~66%/yr; BTC Sharpe ~0.8. Alexander & Imeraj (2021) built the Bitcoin VIX from 7M+ Deribit prices (Mar 2019-2020) and document a large, time-varying BVRP that spikes before big moves. Funding-rate carry (cash-and-carry: long spot / short perp): ~10-19% annualized in average conditions, positive the large majority of 8h windows, compressing toward zero as capital enters.
- Strength: moderate · Recency: Most current crypto evidence (2021-2024); but small samples, exchange/counterparty risk (FTX), and funding compresses fast when crowded. BVRP decoupled from equities pre-COVID, then correlated during COVID.
- Cites: Almeida, Grith, Miftachov & Wang 2024, 'Risk Premia in the Bitcoin Market', arXiv:2410.15195; Alexander & Imeraj 2021, 'The Bitcoin VIX and Its Variance Risk Premium', Journal of Alternative Investments / SSRN 3383734; Almeida et al. citing Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou 2009 (S&P 2% VRP) and Martin 2017 (equity premium ~5%)

**The cross-section of single-name delta-hedged option returns is unconditionally negative (sellers earn the premium), with a common variance-risk factor — the original Carr-Wu / Coval-Shumway evidence — but single-name premia are noisier and costlier to harvest than index.**
- Effect size: Carr & Wu (2009): average ATM straddle returns and delta-hedged call/put returns large and unconditionally negative; zero-beta ATM straddles lose ~3%/week (Coval-Shumway). Index VRP much larger and more systematic than most single names (only some names show significant premium).
- Strength: moderate · Recency: Foundational (2001-2009); the index-vs-single-name gap and the post-2010 decay both reduce the harvestable single-name edge; transaction costs on single-name options are materially higher.
- Cites: Carr & Wu 2009, 'Variance Risk Premia', RFS 22(3); Coval & Shumway 2001, 'Expected Option Returns', Journal of Finance 56(3); Bakshi & Kapadia 2003, RFS (delta-hedged gains)

### Testable hypotheses
- H1 (CRYPTO VRP, primary): Using Deribit BTC/ETH IV surfaces + DVOL (2021-2026), a strategy that sells 1-week to 1-month ATM straddles/strangles (or short variance via the DVOL/var-swap formula) when DVOL > trailing 20-30d realized vol earns a positive gross premium; test whether net-of-cost (Deribit taker fee 0.03% of underlying capped, plus bid-ask) Sharpe stays > 0.5 and whether it survives the largest DVOL spikes in-sample. Predicted: gross VRP ~10-15 vol-pts annualized, net Sharpe positive but heavily tail-exposed.
- H2 (FUNDING CARRY = short-vol analog, primary): On the 228-perp x ~23k-hour funding dataset + Coinalyze, a delta-neutral long-spot/short-perp (or short-perp when funding>threshold) carry earns funding that is positive in the large majority of 8h windows; test net Sharpe after fees+slippage, and CRITICALLY test conditional behavior during liquidation cascades (Coinalyze liquidations) — does the carry's worst drawdowns cluster exactly with funding sign-flips and OI unwinds (the crypto 'Volmageddon')? Predicted positive carry ~10-19%/yr that compresses over 2024-2026 as the trade crowds.
- H3 (DECAY / regime, equity): Reconstruct a monthly ATM SPX-proxy short-straddle and delta-hedged short-put on our 1yr S&P 500 daily/15m bars (using listed-option proxies once option data sourced); test the Dew-Becker-Giglio claim that alpha ~0 post-2020 by comparing pre/post-2020 mean returns and t-stats. Predicted: gross premium positive but alpha indistinguishable from zero after costs; falsified if t-stat of net alpha > 2.
- H4 (VRP as a CONDITIONING signal, not a standalone trade): Test Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou predictability on DVOL — does (DVOL^2 - realized variance) predict next 1-4 week BTC/ETH spot returns with R^2 comparable to the ~15% they found for equities? If yes, VRP is more valuable as an overlay/timing signal than as raw premium collection. Falsifiable via out-of-sample R^2 <= 0.
- H5 (Skew / crash-insurance pricing): Using Deribit IV surfaces, test whether selling the put-wing (25-delta puts) earns a richer risk-adjusted premium than ATM (equity put-skew analog), and whether OTM-put selling has a worse left-tail in BTC drawdowns. Predicted: richer premium but fatter left tail; net Sharpe edge ambiguous.
- H6 (Microstructure realized-vol edge): With 56M SPY/QQQ LOB snapshots + Databento ITCH, build a high-frequency realized-variance forecast; test whether a better RV nowcast lets a short-vol position systematically avoid selling when forward RV will exceed IV (i.e., turn the negative-skew lottery into a conditioned trade). Falsified if forecast adds no net-of-cost improvement over a naive trailing-RV rule (consistent with arXiv 2506.07928 'can anything beat the benchmark').

### Harvest strategies
- CRYPTO short straddle/strangle (Deribit BTC/ETH): sell 1-week ATM straddle or 16-25 delta strangle, delta-hedge with perp daily. Cost drag: Deribit option fee 0.03% of underlying (capped at 12.5% of premium) per side + ~0.03% perp fee for hedging + bid-ask (wider than SPX, can be 1-3 vol pts on weeklies). Net edge plausible given ~14% BVRP but tail must be capped (buy a far OTM wing or hard stop). This is the single most testable VRP trade on our data.
- CRYPTO funding-rate carry (delta-neutral): long spot (or long-dated future) + short perp on coins where funding is persistently positive; collect funding every 8h. Cost drag: ~2x taker/maker fees on entry+exit + borrow/spot custody + slippage; net ~5-12%/yr after costs in calm regimes, but size for the cascade event where funding flips and basis blows out. Directly uses our 228-perp funding + Coinalyze OI/liquidation data.
- CRYPTO DVOL-conditioned variance selling: short variance (replicate via strip of options per the var-swap formula, or short DVOL futures if accessible) only when DVOL premium over trailing RV is in the top tercile. Cost drag: full option-strip rebalancing is expensive in crypto (wide spreads); a coarse short-strangle proxy is more cost-realistic.
- EQUITY put-write (benchmark/control, NOT alpha): replicate PUT/WPUT on SPX once option data sourced — sell ATM monthly/weekly puts cash-secured in T-bills. Cost drag: ~5-10 bps/round-trip commission + bid-ask + market impact; realistic net Sharpe ~0.4-0.5 historically and ~0 post-2020. Use as a cost/decay reality-check, not as the edge.
- RISK-MANAGED covered call (Israelov-style): if running equity short-vol, strip the uncompensated equity-reversal leg by delta-hedging the embedded short-call exposure — improves Sharpe and cuts downside beta vs naive covered call. Cost drag: extra daily delta hedging in the underlying (small for liquid SPY/QQQ).
- TAIL OVERLAY (mandatory for any short-vol book): finance a cheap convex hedge (far-OTM puts / long-vol wing) sized to survive a Feb-2018/Mar-2020-magnitude move; accept it lowers gross Sharpe but prevents ruin. The historical record (XIV -96%) shows un-hedged levered short-vol is uninvestable.

### Pitfalls
- SURVIVORSHIP / peso-problem on the tail: the headline Sharpes (0.65-1.0) are computed over samples whose worst tail (or the un-survived products like XIV) is under-weighted. Negative skew (-2.09) and kurtosis (12.6) mean Sharpe massively overstates true risk-adjusted attractiveness; use Sortino/Stutzer, CVaR, and explicit max-loss-to-ruin, not Sharpe.
- GROSS-vs-NET illusion: nearly every attractive number cited (AQR 0.68, CBOE PUT 0.65, covered-call short-vol leg ~1.0) is GROSS of execution costs and is an INDEX construct that bundles a T-bill or equity-beta carry leg. The investable PUTW ETF netted only 8.34%/yr vs S&P 13.27% over 10yr. Always isolate the pure delta-hedged option P&L net of bid-ask + commissions + hedging costs.
- DECAY / non-stationarity: the equity VRP alpha converged to ~zero by 2020 (Dew-Becker-Giglio) and rolling VRP went negative 2023-2024. Backtests spanning 1986-2016 are dominated by a regime that no longer exists; weight recent sub-periods and test for structural breaks. Do NOT extrapolate pre-2010 Sharpes.
- DATA-SNOOPING / multiple testing: short-vol has thousands of degrees of freedom (DTE, strike/delta, entry filter, stop level, hedge ratio, rebalance frequency). Harvey-Liu-Zhu (2016) argue t>3.0 is the right hurdle for a 'new' factor after multiple testing — apply it; a strangle backtest with Sharpe 2.2 (the earnings-straddle example) is almost certainly overfit once costs and the search space are accounted.
- SELECTION ON THE WINNING SIDE: spintwig finds the CALL side of SPX strangles is systematically unprofitable — short-vol P&L is asymmetric and side-dependent; aggregate strangle stats hide that the put side carries the premium and the tail.
- CRYPTO-SPECIFIC: tiny samples (Deribit options liquid only since ~2019-2021), exchange/counterparty risk (FTX collapse wiped out 'risk-free' carry), funding caps and fee tiers, and rapid premium compression as capital crowds in 2024-2026. Backtested crypto VRP Sharpes will be optimistically biased by the absence of a realized exchange-failure event in-sample.
- AUTOCORRELATED / illiquid marks: option and var-swap returns have stale/smoothed marks that depress measured vol and inflate Sharpe; the 'strong serial correlation in large negative days' (Quantpedia) means daily Sharpe is not annualizable by sqrt(252). Use realized close-out P&L, not mark-to-model.
- CAPACITY & feedback: short-vol has limited capacity precisely because crowding creates the feedback loop that causes the crash (leveraged ETPs' VIX-futures share drove Volmageddon). Strategy capacity is regime-dependent and shrinks exactly when you most want to exit.

### Data needed
- HAVE (use now): Deribit BTC/ETH IV surfaces + DVOL 2021-2026 (for crypto straddle/variance VRP, H1/H4/H5); 228 perps x ~23k h funding history + Coinalyze funding/OI/liquidations (for funding-carry H2 and crash-clustering); top-50 OHLCV 1h/4h/1d for realized-vol computation; SPY/QQQ LOB + Databento ITCH (for HF realized-vol nowcast H6).
- NEED — equity option data (FREE sources): CBOE index history (PUT, BXM, WPUT, BXMD, PPUT, VIX) free from Cboe.com index pages and FRED (VIXCLS, and Cboe publishes daily index levels); VIX futures settlement history free from Cboe; for actual SPX/SPY option chains historically the free options are limited — use (a) Cboe DataShop sample/free index files, (b) ORATS/historicaloptiondata.com free samples, (c) Dolthub free options datasets, (d) yfinance for recent live chains. OptionMetrics (the academic standard) is paid via WRDS — only if accessible through GaTech.
- NEED — realized-variance / VRP series: construct VIX-minus-realized directly from VIXCLS (FRED) + SPX returns; for crypto build the var-swap-fair-value index from Deribit chains per Alexander-Imeraj / Cboe VIX methodology.
- NEED — crypto option fee/borrow schedule: Deribit fee tiers (taker 0.03% of underlying, capped 12.5% of premium), perp funding caps, and spot borrow rates — to model net-of-cost P&L honestly.
- NICE-TO-HAVE: SVXY/VXX/UVXY price history (free, Yahoo/Stooq) to study levered short-vol product decay and the Feb-2018 event; intraday VIX for the Feb 5 2018 reconstruction.
- NOT NEEDED for this area: FX/commodities term structure (those are separate carry studies); large GPU/model capacity — per prior finding, edge is the anomaly + cost/tail rigor, not model size. A clean event-aware backtester with realistic fills matters far more than the H100s here.

### Crypto/recent notes
CRYPTO IS WHERE THE LIVE EDGE PLAUSIBLY REMAINS, and it maps cleanly to our data. Bitcoin VRP ~14%/yr (Almeida et al. 2024, arXiv:2410.15195) is ~7x the ~2% S&P 500 VRP; Alexander & Imeraj (2021, SSRN 3383734) built the Bitcoin VIX from Deribit and document a large, time-varying premium that spikes before big moves. We can test crypto straddle/variance selling directly on Deribit DVOL + IV surfaces (2021-2026), and the perp funding rate (~10-19%/yr, positive most 8h windows, compressing as capital enters) is an economically identical short-vol/insurance carry testable on our 228-perp funding + Coinalyze liquidation data — including the crucial test of whether carry drawdowns cluster with funding sign-flips and liquidation cascades (the crypto analog of Volmageddon). RECENT-EQUITY CAVEAT (decisive): Dew-Becker & Giglio (2025, Chicago Fed WP 2025-17 / SSRN 5525882) show delta-hedged put and ATM-straddle alphas converged to ZERO by ~2020 (straddles pre-COVID), synthetic options >90% correlated with traded ones, consistent with an intermediary story not a free anomaly; the 12-month rolling equity VRP went negative in 2023-2024. So in liquid US equity/VIX markets the cash VRP is largely a paper artifact post-2020 once realistic costs and the negatively-skewed tail (XIV -96%, SVXY -80% Feb 5 2018; PUTW -28% Mar 2020) are honestly priced. Treat equity put-write/covered-call as a COST-AND-DECAY CONTROL, prioritize CRYPTO VRP + funding carry as the falsifiable live bets, and never run short-vol unhedged or unbounded — size for ruin, not for Sharpe.

### Adversarial verification — reliability: **medium**
_Net-of-cost reality:_ Blunt take: in liquid US equity/VIX markets the cash VRP is now a weak-to-dead edge, and the review's own bottom line is essentially correct. The decay finding is real, primary-sourced, and decisive (Dew-Becker & Giglio 2025: delta-hedged put and ATM-straddle alphas indistinguishable from zero; synthetic options >90% correlated with traded; intermediary-frictions story) — and the break is ~2010, OLDER than the review implies, so any backtest leaning on pre-2010 data is mis-stating the live regime. The headline 0.65-1.0 Sharpes are gross, index-level, and bundle a T-bill/beta carry leg; the investable proof (PUT index ~8.0% vs S&P ~10.7% over 10yr; PUTW worse) shows the edge does not survive fees, bid-ask, or bull-market opportunity cost. Tail risk is structural and recurring (XIV ~-96%, SVXY ~-80% in 2018; vol funds -40% in a single day on Aug 5 2024 with VIX at 65.73) — Sharpe materially overstates attractiveness given skew ~-2 and kurtosis ~12. The one genuine refinement is that POST-2018 de-levered, risk-managed, hedged short-vol (e.g. SVOL ~-13% in Aug 2024, no blow-up) is survivable, which supports the review's 'size for ruin, run a tail overlay' prescription over naive premium collection. The crypto pivot is where the review is most exposed: the ~14% BVRP / ~66% BP / ~0.8 Sharpe numbers are accurately cited but are UNCONDITIONAL, risk-neutral-density estimates with NO net-of-cost harvesting backtest, the premium is ~39% right-tail-driven (a short-vol seller does not cleanly capture it), and the economically-equivalent funding carry just FAILED its first real stress test — the October 2025 cascade (funding 10%->30% then collapse, basis 6.9%->4.5%, ~$154B liquidated, 'hedge became a loss amplifier'), with December-2025 BTC basis ~4.46% and ~93% of days below the ~5% breakeven, i.e. net-negative carry most days. Net: treat equity put-write/covered-call as a cost-and-decay control (correct), but downgrade the crypto VRP/funding 'standout live edge' from a conclusion to an unproven, heavily tail-exposed and now visibly-crowded hypothesis. Across the board the live, net-of-cost, post-crowding edge is far thinner than any of the headline academic Sharpes suggest.
- **[CONFIRMED]** DECAY IS THE DOMINANT FINDING: equity VRP / delta-hedged option alpha has collapsed to ~zero; delta-hedged put and ATM-straddle alphas converged by ~2020 (straddles pre-COVID); synthetic options >90% correlated with traded options; intermediary-frictions explanation (Dew-Becker & Giglio 2025). — Independently verified against the primary source (Chicago Fed WP 2025-17 / dew-becker.org). The paper states option alphas have become 'indistinguishable from zero' over the past ~15 years, that synthetic option returns are 'over 90 percent correlated' with traded option returns, and that an intermediary-based model explains the decline. The convergence for ATM straddles came 'even before Covid,' and 'as of January 2020 the difference in rolling information ratios was no longer significant.' One nuance that STRENGTHENS the adversarial case: the structural break is dated to ~2010 ('over the past 15 years'), older and more established than the finding's '~2020' emphasis implies — so the pre-2010 Sharpes are even less representative of the current regime than stated. This is the single most decisive, well-sourced claim in the review and it cuts directly against the headline 0.65-1.0 Sharpe narrative.
- **[WEAKENED]** CRYPTO VRP IS THE STANDOUT LIVE OPPORTUNITY: Bitcoin 1-month VRP ~14%/yr (~7x the ~2% S&P VRP), BTC return premium ~66%/yr, Sharpe ~0.8 (Almeida, Grith, Miftachov & Wang 2024); perp funding carry ~10-19%/yr is an economically identical, harvestable short-vol/insurance premium. — The cited numbers are accurate to the source: the arXiv:2410.15195 paper (Aug 2025 v2) states BVRP averages ~14% and BP ~66% per annum for a 1-month horizon, BTC annualized Sharpe ~0.8 (~2x S&P), and explicitly contrasts with Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou's ~2% S&P VRP and Martin's ~5% equity-premium lower bound. BUT the 'standout LIVE/harvestable opportunity' framing is overstated on three counts. (1) These are UNCONDITIONAL premia estimated from risk-neutral densities — the paper reports NO backtested net-of-cost short-vol strategy, no bid-ask, no Deribit fee modeling; the 0.8 Sharpe is the BTC ASSET Sharpe, not a short-vol-strategy Sharpe. (2) The paper itself shows ~39% of the Bitcoin premium comes from large POSITIVE (right-tail) returns and only ~1/3 from the -1 to -3 sigma left tail — a short-straddle/short-vol seller is short the right tail too, so it does NOT cleanly capture the 14% BVRP / 66% BP. (3) The funding-carry analog has just been stress-tested live and largely failed (see next claim). So the academic premium is real and large, but its translation into a harvestable, net-of-cost short-vol edge is unproven and the optimism is a leap beyond the evidence.
- **[WEAKENED]** Perp funding-rate carry (delta-neutral long-spot/short-perp) earns ~10-19%/yr, positive most 8h windows, 'compressing as capital enters' but a live edge; worst drawdowns hypothesized to cluster with funding sign-flips/liquidation cascades (the crypto Volmageddon, H2). — The carry's existence and the predicted crowding/compression are confirmed, but the live-edge optimism is undermined by an event the findings entirely MISS (their data ends ~2024). The crypto 'Volmageddon' the analyst only HYPOTHESIZED actually occurred in October 2025: funding had run from ~10% to ~30% annualized into early Oct 2025, then the cascade hit and basis compressed from 6.9% to 4.5%, funding flipped negative, and the delta-neutral 'hedge became a loss amplifier' — a 15% spot drop with 2.4% basis compression implied ~15.6% loss on a 'hedged' book; ~$154B was liquidated in crypto in 2025. By December 2025 front-month BTC basis had collapsed to ~4.46% with ~93% of trading days below the ~5% breakeven, i.e. the carry was net-negative most days after costs. So the trade is real in calm regimes but (a) compresses below breakeven when crowded and (b) carries exactly the cascade/ruin tail the analyst flagged — confirming the pitfall while refuting the 'standout live edge' tone. One caveat: a separate promotional exchange source claimed funding-arb returns ROSE to ~19% in 2025 with <1% drawdown — this is self-interested and inconsistent with the independent market-structure reporting, so I down-weight it.
- **[CONFIRMED]** TAIL RISK / RUIN is the defining feature: Feb 5 2018 Volmageddon destroyed inverse-VIX ETPs via a forced-buying feedback loop (XIV -96%, SVXY >-80%); this is a structural, repeating hazard whenever short-vol notional and crowding are high. — Mechanism and magnitudes independently verified: XIV fell ~96-97% and was terminated under its <20% acceleration-event clause; SVXY fell ~80-91% (sources differ); ETP managers had to buy ~$4B of VIX futures into evaporating liquidity, a self-reinforcing feedback loop. The 'repeats when crowding is high' claim is also borne out: Aug 5 2024 saw VIX spike to an intraday 65.73 (largest one-day VIX jump on record) and vol-strategy funds reportedly lost up to 40% in a single day. IMPORTANT REFINEMENT that the findings under-state: the SAME Aug 2024 stress did NOT wipe out modern 1x/levered short-vol ETPs — post-2018 de-levering worked. The risk-managed SVOL (-0.2 to -0.3x VIX-futures, with hedges) drew down only ~13% despite VIX +308% intraday. This both confirms the ruin hazard for naive/levered exposure AND validates the review's own 'risk-managed sizing / tail overlay' thesis: ruin is a feature of leverage and crowding, not of bounded, hedged short-vol per se.
- **[CONFIRMED]** Headline put-write Sharpes (CBOE PUT 0.65, 1986-2018; AQR beta-hedged short-options 0.68, 1996-2016) are gross of costs and INDEX constructs bundling a T-bill/equity-carry leg; the edge did NOT translate to live net-of-cost outperformance (PUTW ~8.3%/yr vs S&P ~13.3% over 10yr). — Independent sources confirm both the historical index edge AND its failure to survive live/net-of-cost. Cboe/Bondarenko figures (PUT 1986-2018: ~9.5% return, ~10% vol, Sharpe ~0.65, skew -2.09, kurtosis ~12.6, max DD -32.7%) are widely reproduced. More decisively for the adversarial case: the INVESTABLE record lags badly — the CBOE PUT index 10yr annualized is ~8.0% vs S&P 500 TR ~10.7% (as of ~mid-2025), and the PUTW ETF (0.44% fee, 2018 -7.1%, 2022 -10.1%) underperformed the S&P by ~4-5 pts/yr over a decade. Exact figures (8.34% vs 13.27%, or 7.2%) vary by data vendor and as-of date, but the direction and magnitude of the gap are robustly confirmed. The 'gross-of-cost, bundled-carry-leg, index-not-investable' critique is the correct frame and is well-supported. AQR's own white paper does state its 0.68 is 'gross of transaction costs and fees.'

---

## Crypto volatility and VRP (Deribit, DVOL)  `crypto_vol`

The crypto variance risk premium (VRP) is real, large, and the same sign as equities: implied vol persistently exceeds realized, so the SHORT-vol side earns the premium (a "negative VRP" in the academic implied-minus-realized convention, equivalently positive carry to sellers). On Deribit, 30-day BTC implied has exceeded 30-day realized ~70% of the time since 2019, with a median premium of ~+14 vol points and an annualized variance-swap VRP of ~14% (Almeida et al. 2025) versus ~2% for the S&P 500 (Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou) — so in raw magnitude crypto VRP is ~7x equities, but it is NOT a free lunch: it is compensation for far higher realized vol (~55-80% ann), fat tails, and crash risk, and gross Sharpes (delta-hedged short straddles/risk-reversals ~1-2 in 2019-2022 backtests) compress materially after Deribit fees, bid-ask, weekly delta-hedge slippage, and inventory/funding costs. Crucially the edge is decaying and regime-dependent: institutionalization (Jan-2024 spot ETFs, Nov-2024 IBIT options reaching ~$53B OI vs Deribit ~$50B by Dec-2025) compressed IV toward ~32% (vs 50% 1-yr avg) and converged TradFi/crypto skew to <0.2 pts by Sep-2025; crypto carry Sharpe collapsed from 6.45 (2020-24) to 4.06 (2024) to negative in 2025 (Borri et al. 2026); the equity VRP itself has decayed to ~zero alpha since ~2010 (Dew-Becker-Giglio 2025), a likely template for crypto. Naive short-vol "blew up" in March-2020/May-2021/June-2022/Nov-2022 and ETH VRP went outright negative (realized > implied) in early-2025. Net: a survivable but shrinking, actively-managed premium — passive covered-call/short-straddle selling has historically LOST money net (Liberty Road passive CC: -9.79% ann, Sharpe -0.54).

### Findings

**BTC variance risk premium is large and the SAME sign as equities (implied > realized; short side earns it). Annualized variance-swap VRP ~14% (risk-neutral var 0.72 vs physical 0.58) vs ~2% for S&P 500 — roughly 7x in raw magnitude. Return premium (BP) ~66%/yr but BTC standalone Sharpe only ~0.8 (~2x S&P's 0.5).**
- Effect size: BVRP = sigma_Q^2 - sigma_P^2 = 0.72 - 0.58 = 0.14 annualized (one-month horizon); regime-split 0.12 high-vol / 0.17 low-vol. S&P500 VRP ~0.02 (Bollerslev-Tauchen-Zhou 2009). BTC BP ~66%/yr, SR ~0.8. Note: 'negative VRP' in implied-minus-realized convention = positive carry to sellers.
- Strength: strong · Recency: Sample Jul-2017 to Dec-2022 (Deribit). Magnitude robust across multiple papers; sign (large positive premium to sellers) confirmed by Atanasova et al. on Jan-2020-Jul-2024 data. But level has compressed post-2024 (see decay finding).
- Cites: Almeida, Grith, Miftachov & Wang 2025, 'Risk Premia in the Bitcoin Market', arXiv:2410.15195v2; Bollerslev, Tauchen & Zhou 2009, RFS (S&P500 VRP ~2% baseline); Martin 2017 QJE (S&P EP lower bound ~5%)

**On Deribit, 30-day BTC implied vol has exceeded 30-day realized ~70% of the time since Apr-2019; median VRP ~+14 IV points. This is the core harvestable structural edge and it is positive far more often than negative.**
- Effect size: IV>RV ~70% of time (since Apr-2019). Median VRP +14 vol points; 25th pctile +1.80; 5th pctile -20; min/max ~±70 vol points. In contango term-structure regime mean VRP ~+15 pts; in backwardation mean negative with wide distribution.
- Strength: strong · Recency: Practitioner data through 2023; consistent with academic samples through mid-2024. The +14 median is unconditional and pre-cost.
- Cites: Deribit Insights, 'Decoding Option Flows: Q2 2023'; Deribit Insights, 'Bitcoin Options: Finding edge in four years of volatility regimes'

**Delta-hedged crypto option returns are strongly positive to sellers and economically very large; BTC volatility risk premium (implied-minus-realized) is 'consistently negative and significantly larger than' equities (i.e., bigger seller carry). Plus a positive illiquidity premium for selling illiquid options.**
- Effect size: Average DAILY delta-hedged option return ~0.24% (Atanasova et al., Jan-2020-Jul-2024, Deribit, BTC). +1 SD option illiquidity adds ~0.07%/day (calls), 0.06%/day (puts) to delta-hedged returns; illiquidity premium ~0.17% per contract. Hedging/rebalancing cost proxies explain ~60% of cross-sectional variation. Deribit = ~80% BTC option volume, ~90% OI.
- Strength: strong · Recency: Jan-2020 to Jul-2024 — includes 2022 bear and 2024 ETF era; premium persisted but the 0.24%/day is GROSS of taker fees and spreads and includes a tail-risk-bearing component.
- Cites: Atanasova et al., 'Illiquidity Premium and Crypto Option Returns', AUT/ACFR working paper (Deribit BTC, 2020-2024); Sepp & Lucic 2024, 'Valuation and hedging of cryptocurrency inverse options', Quantitative Finance 24(7); Bakshi & Kapadia 2003 RFS (foundational negative vol risk premium / delta-hedged gains)

**Systematic short-vol structures (delta-hedged weekly short straddle, short risk-reversal) showed strong GROSS risk-adjusted performance 2019-2022, with short risk-reversal best; mean-variance optimal portfolios put 75-90% weight on the short-vol leg + spot BTC.**
- Effect size: Weekly short straddle (delta-hedged after each 2.5% move): max-Sharpe portfolio ~90% straddle + 10% spot. Short risk-reversal: best risk-adjusted, robust across delta thresholds, optimal ~75-80% weight; aided by negative spot-vol correlation present ~65% of time. Sold butterflies underperformed (theta drag from long legs). Sharpe figures qualitative ('strong'); no published net-of-cost SR.
- Strength: moderate · Recency: Backtest 2019-05 to 2022-12 (Deribit). Pre-cost, in-sample optimized; no out-of-sample or net-of-fee Sharpe disclosed — treat allocations as upper bounds.
- Cites: Deribit Insights, 'Bitcoin Options: Finding edge in four years of volatility regimes'; Alexander & Imeraj 2021, 'The Bitcoin VIX and Its Variance Risk Premium', J. Alternative Investments 23(4)

**PASSIVE crypto vol-selling has historically LOST money; only actively risk-managed, vol-targeted selling produced positive net Sharpe. This is the central honest caveat: the premium does not survive naive harvesting.**
- Effect size: Liberty Road live results: Passive covered calls -9.79%/yr, Sharpe -0.54; a competing 'Active' fund -32.86%/yr, Sharpe -1.65; semi-active +5.07%/yr; only the EVaR vol-targeted (5% vol) 'Treasury' product +9.90%/yr, Sharpe +1.76 — NET of 2% mgmt + 20% perf fees. Active risk mgmt added ~+20% to risk-adjusted returns.
- Strength: moderate · Recency: Live 2021-2023 results (post-2020). Demonstrates regime/risk-management dependence; small-N live track records.
- Cites: LibertyRoad Capital 2023, 'Covered Call Strategies in the Bitcoin Options/Volatility Markets'

**Crypto VRP/carry is DECAYING fast with institutionalization. Spot ETFs (Jan-2024) + IBIT options (Nov-2024) created a parallel regulated market that converged with Deribit; IV compressed and the crypto carry Sharpe collapsed and turned negative in 2025.**
- Effect size: Crypto carry annualized Sharpe 6.45 (2020-25) -> 4.06 (from 2024) -> NEGATIVE in 2025 (Borri et al. 2026). Avg cross-exchange carry ~7%/yr (Apr-2019-Jul-2024); BTC 1m basis ~6.4-8%, spikes >40-55%. IBIT options OI ~$53.3B vs Deribit ~$50B by Dec-2025; ATM IV tracked closely across venues; crash-skew gap 15.3 pts (Jul-1-2025: IBIT 33.4 vs Deribit 18.1) -> <0.2 pts by Sep-2025. IV fell to ~32% vs ~50% 1-yr avg.
- Strength: moderate · Recency: 2024-2026 — the most current evidence; directly signals the premium is being arbitraged/competed down as the market matures.
- Cites: Borri, Liu et al. 2026, 'Cryptocurrency as an Investable Asset Class: Coming of Age', arXiv:2510.14435v4; Schmeling, Schrimpf & Todorov 2023, 'Crypto carry', BIS WP 1087 / SSRN 4268371; ETF Express 2026-06-11, 'Bitcoin options markets converging across TradFi and Crypto'

**The equity VRP — the template for crypto — has itself decayed to ~zero alpha over the last ~15 years, consistent with synthetic options. This is a strong prior that crypto VRP compresses as intermediation deepens.**
- Effect size: Equity index option alphas ~indistinguishable from zero over past ~15 yrs (break ~2010); previously sharply negative. Short realized-variance claim historically Sharpe ~+1.7 (5x equity SR) but only at the VERY short end of the term structure; longer-dated variance claims earn little. VIX-RV gap averaged 4.2 pts (1990-2018); CBOE PUT index SR 0.65 vs S&P 0.49 (32-yr).
- Strength: strong · Recency: Decline documented through 2025 — explicit warning that VRP strategies decay post-discovery/competition.
- Cites: Dew-Becker & Giglio 2025, 'The Decline of the Variance Risk Premium', Chicago Fed WP 2025-17 / SSRN 5525882; Dew-Becker, Giglio, Le & Rodriguez 2017, 'The Price of Variance Risk', JFE (Sharpe ~-1.7 short end); Carr & Wu 2009, 'Variance Risk Premia', RFS; Cboe/Wilshire 2019, 'Options-Based Benchmark Indexes' & 'Historical Performance of Put-Writing Strategies'

**VRP is regime- and asset-dependent: contango+positive-skew regimes are reliably sellable; backwardation/vol-shocks are where short-vol blows up. ETH VRP can differ from BTC and went NEGATIVE (realized>implied) in early-2025.**
- Effect size: IV>RV ~70% (BTC). Vol shocks spiked term-structure to ~1.45 ratio (Mar-2020, May-2021, Jun-2022, Nov-2022). Jan-2025: BTC ATM IV ~54.2%, ETH ~62.7%; ETH realized ran ~50% higher than BTC but ETH IV priced only ~30% premium -> ETH VRP negative (sellers lost). VRP 'spikes before large +/- returns' (Alexander-Imeraj) and BP-BVRP are NEGATIVELY related in BTC (opposite to equities).
- Strength: moderate · Recency: 2025 data; shows the premium is conditional and that blind selling across regimes/assets is dangerous.
- Cites: Block Scholes, 'Volatility Review January 2025'; Deribit Insights, 'Finding edge in four years of volatility regimes'; Almeida et al. 2025 arXiv:2410.15195 (negative BP-BVRP relation); Alexander & Imeraj 2021

### Testable hypotheses
- H1 (core VRP existence): On our Deribit DVOL + IV-surface data (2021-2026), DVOL_t (30d implied) exceeds subsequent 30d realized vol (close-to-close and Garman-Klass on 1h bars) >65% of months for BTC, with a mean gap of +8 to +14 vol points. Test: paired t-test and sign test on monthly IV-RV; report % positive and mean/median in vol points.
- H2 (decay): The BTC IV-RV gap and DVOL level are structurally LOWER in 2024-02->2026-06 (post-ETF) than 2021->2023, and the gap shrank further after Nov-2024 IBIT options launch. Test: Chow/structural-break and rolling-12m mean of (DVOL - RV) with breakpoints at 2024-01 and 2024-11.
- H3 (short-vol net Sharpe): A delta-hedged weekly short ATM straddle on BTC (hedge after each 2.5% move), 2021-2026, has GROSS annualized Sharpe >1.0 but NET Sharpe (Deribit 0.03%-of-underlying fee capped at 12.5% of premium, plus 1 vol-pt bid-ask, plus hedge slippage on perps at observed funding/spreads) falls by >40% and the maximum drawdown exceeds 30%. Test: full event-driven backtest with our IV surfaces + perp funding history; report gross vs net SR, MaxDD, skew, deflated Sharpe.
- H4 (regime conditioning beats unconditional): Conditioning short-vol entry on contango (front<back DVOL term structure) and positive/neutral risk-reversal skew raises net Sharpe and cuts MaxDD vs always-on selling. Test: compare unconditional vs regime-gated short-straddle/short-RR; out-of-sample split 2021-2023 train / 2024-2026 test.
- H5 (ETH vs BTC): ETH VRP is more volatile and turns negative more often than BTC; specifically ETH had negative VRP (realized>implied) in early-2025. Test: replicate H1 on ETH DVOL, compare % positive and tail months to BTC; flag 2025 episodes.
- H6 (perp funding as a vol/VRP signal): Standardized perp funding rate and OI changes (Coinalyze, 228 perps x 23k hrs) predict next-week realized vol and the sign of the realized VRP; extreme positive funding precedes vol spikes that hurt short-vol. Test: predictive regressions of fwd RV and short-straddle PnL on lagged funding/OI/liquidations; report IC and hit rate.
- H7 (DVOL futures basis / VRP term structure): The DVOL term structure (or DVOL-vs-RV) predicts the cross-section of short-vol PnL by tenor; weekly straddles dominate monthly on a Sharpe basis as Deribit research suggests. Test: compare 1w vs 1m vs 1q delta-hedged short-vol Sharpes on our data.
- H8 (cross-asset cousin we CAN run cheaply): The same short-vol logic applied to SPY/QQQ via VIX and 0DTE-style short straddles on our S&P 500 15m/1h bars yields a smaller but positive net premium (SR ~0.4-0.7, per Cboe PUT), confirming crypto VRP is larger-but-not-uniquely-efficient; use as a benchmark for whether crypto edge is just beta-of-vol.

### Harvest strategies
- S1 — Delta-hedged weekly short ATM straddle (BTC, then ETH): Sell 1w ATM call+put on Deribit, hedge delta with BTC perp after each ~2.5% move, roll weekly. This is the canonical VRP harvester; Deribit research found ~90% straddle + 10% spot maximizes Sharpe 2019-2022. Cost drag: Deribit option fee 0.03% of underlying notional per leg (capped at 12.5% of premium) -> ~0.06% round-trip-equivalent per leg; combo discount waives the cheaper leg's taker fee; plus ~0.5-1.5 vol-pt bid-ask on the straddle; plus perp delta-hedge slippage + funding (use our 228-perp funding history to model realistically). Net edge survives ONLY with vol-targeting and regime gating.
- S2 — Short risk-reversal (sell rich wing): Deribit research found short RR offers the best risk-adjusted return and is robust to delta choice; sell the more expensive wing (in 2021 sell puts/buy calls when call-skew rich; in 2022 sell calls/buy puts when put-skew rich), delta-hedged. Lower theta/gamma footprint than straddle; cost drag dominated by one extra option leg + hedging.
